				function __gtagTrackerIsOptedOut() {

						if (document.cookie.indexOf(disableStrs[index] + '=true') > -1) {
							return true;
						}
					}

					}
				}

	<div class="post-372 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-minimalism entry"><h1 class="entry-title">How to Start a Successful Blog in 2023</h1>
<div class="post-info">By <span class="author vcard"><span class="fn"><a href="https://www.theminimalists.com/about/#jfm" rel="author external">Joshua Fields Millburn</a></span></span>  <span class="follow-links">Follow: <a href="https://facebook.com/theminimalists" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Facebook</a>, <a href="https://twitter.com/JFM" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Twitter</a>, <a href="https://instagram.com/joshuafieldsmillburn" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Instagram</a></span> <span class="updated_wrap">Updated <span class="date updated time" title="2023-02-18T00:33:16-05:00">February 18, 2023</span></span></div><div class="entry-content"><p>Learn how to start a blog in less than an hour. Become a blogger today by following the steps we used when starting our blog, which now has reached more than 20 million people and has been seen in the <em>New York Times</em>, TIME magazine, and on the TODAY show.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" style="border: 1px solid #eee; box-sizing: border-box; margin: 5px 0;" src="./How to Start a Successful Blog in 2023 - The Minimalists_files/how-to-start-a-blog-in-2020.jpg" alt="How to Start a Blog in 2023" width="500" height="281" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/how-to-start-a-blog-in-2020.jpg" data-ll-status="loaded" class="entered lazyloaded"><noscript><img decoding="async" style="border: 1px solid #eee; box-sizing: border-box; margin: 5px 0;" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/how-to-start-a-blog-in-2020.jpg" alt="How to Start a Blog in 2023" width="500" height="281" /></noscript></p>
<h2>How to Become a Blogger in 5 Simple Steps</h2>
<ol>
<li>Choose your blog name and get your blog hosting.</li>
<li>Start your blog by adding WordPress.</li>
<li>Pick a simple theme to make your blog your own.</li>
<li>Add two key blogging plugins to find your readers and track stats.</li>
<li>Write compelling content to create a blog that your readers love.</li>
</ol>
<div id="quick-start" class="quick-start">
<h2>Do you want to start a blog fast?</h2>
<p>This is a long essay and you may want to start your blog without learning all the details.</p>
<p>This is the first how to quickly start a blog guidepost.</p>
<p class="no-margin-bottom"><strong><em>To start a blog fast</em></strong> simply:</p>
<ol>
<li>Look for these boxes.</li>
<li>Follow the brief steps.</li>
<li>Click the link to jump to the next box.</li>
</ol>
<p><a href="https://www.heavytowingtampa.com/">towing in tampa</a> to go to the first step.</p>
</div>
<hr class="narrow">
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter entered lazyloaded" src="./How to Start a Successful Blog in 2023 - The Minimalists_files/how-the-minimalists-started-their-blog.jpg" alt="How The Minimalists started their blog" width="1000" height="667" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/how-the-minimalists-started-their-blog.jpg" data-ll-status="loaded"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/how-the-minimalists-started-their-blog.jpg" alt="How The Minimalists started their blog" width="1000" height="667" /></noscript></p>
<h2 id="how-we-started">How We Started This Blog</h2>
<p>Want to create something meaningful? Why not start a blog? Why not become a blogger? Creating this blog is one of the best decisions Ryan and I ever made. After all, <strong>our blog is how we earn a living</strong>. More important, its how we add value to other peoples lives.</p>
<p>So youre thinking about starting a blog, but you dont have any idea where to start, right? Guess whatneither did we! Before we became The Minimalists, we wanted to start a blog to communicate our thoughts and express our feelings, but we were overwhelmed with options.</p>
<p>Clueless, confused, and confounded with choices, we had no idea how to start a blog or how to be a blogger. When should we start? How do we register a domain name? What is hosting? Which blogging platform should we use? How do we choose a blog theme? What is a plugin? What should we write about? Heck, we could hardly spell HTML, let alone build a blog!</p>
<p>But good news: it turns out that starting a blog is much easier than you think. Weve learned a ton of lessons during our ascent to millions of readers, and now you can learn from our pain and suffering to avoid much of the tedium involved in setting up a blog.</p>
<div class="note"><strong>Disclosure:</strong> <em>The Minimalists</em> blog is hosted by <a href="https://bluehost.sjv.io/Vy9MJJ" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Bluehost</a>. For $2.95 a month, Bluehost can help you set up and host your blog. Because The Minimalists are a Bluehost affiliate partner (i.e., we earn some revenue, at no additional cost to you, when you purchase using our links), our readers can use <a href="https://bluehost.sjv.io/Vy9MJJ" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">this link</a> to receive an over <strong>50% discount off the monthly price and a free domain</strong> for the first year.</div>
<hr class="narrow">
<h2 id="blog-video">How to Become a Blogger: Video Tutorial</h2>
<p>If you prefer to watch our process for setting up a blog, weve created a step-by-step instructional video, <a href="https://youtu.be/Ysf0smDAHhw" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">How to Become a Successful Blogger Today</a>, which shows the entire starting-a-blog undertaking. Otherwise, read on.</p>
<div class="responsive-video">
<span class="embed-youtube" style="text-align:center; display: block;"><div class="rll-youtube-player" data-src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Ysf0smDAHhw" data-id="Ysf0smDAHhw" data-query="version=3&amp;rel=1&amp;showsearch=0&amp;showinfo=1&amp;iv_load_policy=1&amp;fs=1&amp;hl=en-US&amp;autohide=2&amp;wmode=transparent"><div data-id="Ysf0smDAHhw" data-query="version=3&amp;rel=1&amp;showsearch=0&amp;showinfo=1&amp;iv_load_policy=1&amp;fs=1&amp;hl=en-US&amp;autohide=2&amp;wmode=transparent" data-src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Ysf0smDAHhw"><img data-lazy-src="https://i.ytimg.com/vi/Ysf0smDAHhw/hqdefault.jpg" alt="" width="480" height="360" data-ll-status="loaded" class="entered lazyloaded" src="./How to Start a Successful Blog in 2023 - The Minimalists_files/hqdefault.jpg"><noscript><img src="https://i.ytimg.com/vi/ID/hqdefault.jpg" alt="" width="480" height="360"></noscript><button class="play" aria-label="play Youtube video"></button></div></div><noscript><iframe class="youtube-player" width="640" height="360" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Ysf0smDAHhw?version=3&#038;rel=1&#038;showsearch=0&#038;showinfo=1&#038;iv_load_policy=1&#038;fs=1&#038;hl=en-US&#038;autohide=2&#038;wmode=transparent" allowfullscreen="true" style="border:0;" sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-popups allow-presentation"></iframe></noscript></span><br>
</div>
<hr class="narrow">
<h2 id="starting-a-blog-in-depth">How to Start a Successful Blog in 5 Steps</h2>
<ol>
<li>Choose your blog name and get your blog hosting.</li>
<li>Start your blog by adding WordPress.</li>
<li>Pick a simple theme to make your blog your own.</li>
<li>Add two key blogging plugins to find your readers and track stats.</li>
<li>Write compelling content to create a blog that your readers love.</li>
</ol>
<p>While there are other blogging platforms out there like Blogger.com and Tumblr.com, nearly every serious blogger uses a self-hosted WordPress site because of its creative freedom and flexibility.</p>
<p><em>The Minimalists</em> uses WordPress because it gives us greater control over the look and feel of our blogmore creative control than any other platform. Oh, and WordPress itself is <em>free</em>!</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter entered lazyloaded" src="./How to Start a Successful Blog in 2023 - The Minimalists_files/how-to-start-a-blog-in-2020-1.jpg" alt="How to start a blog in 2023" width="1000" height="667" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/how-to-start-a-blog-in-2020-1.jpg" data-ll-status="loaded"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/how-to-start-a-blog-in-2020-1.jpg" alt="How to start a blog in 2023" width="1000" height="667" /></noscript></p>
<p>These are the exact steps we took when we created this website. If you follow these five steps, you will learn how to set up a blog in less than one hour.</p>
<h2 id="start-a-blog-step1" class="start-a-blog-step"><span class="step-highlight">Step 1</span> Choose your blog name and get your blog hosting</h2>
<p>The first thing we did when starting our blog was go to <a href="https://bluehost.sjv.io/Vy9MJJ" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Bluehost</a> and register our domain, which is free with hosting. Well explain hosting in a moment, but lets talk about your domain name first.</p>
<div id="start-fast-1" class="quick-start">
<h3>Blogging Quick Start  Step 1 <p><a href="https://www.heavytowingtampa.com/">towing in tampa</a></h3>
<p>In this first step you will choose your blog name (domain name) and buy your blog hosting.</p>
<ol>
<li>Go to <a href="https://bluehost.sjv.io/Vy9MJJ" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Bluehost</a> and click the <strong><em>Get Started Now</em></strong> button.</li>
<li>Select the <strong><em>Basic plan</em></strong>.</li>
<li>Pick your domain name and enter it into the <strong><em>New Domain</em></strong> box.</li>
<li>Create your Bluehost account.</li>
</ol>
<p><a href="https://www.theminimalists.com/blog/#start-fast-2">Click here</a> to jump to the next step.</p>
</div>
<h3 id="domain-name">Choose your domain name</h3>
<p>Your domain name is an important part of your blog because it creates a first impressionit is the name of your blog. Also known as your URL, your domain is also your address on the web. For example, our domain name is www.theminimalists.com.</p>
<p>So, what do you want to call your blog? Maybe its YourName.com. Maybe its YourBusinessName.com. Or maybe its a creative brand name you thought up. If youre having a hard time thinking of a good domain name, try <a href="http://wordoid.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Wordoid</a>, a wonderful naming tool that will give you plenty of great options. Just make sure you dont buy the domain from them since <a href="https://bluehost.sjv.io/Vy9MJJ" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Bluehost</a> will give you a free domain. (If youve already purchased a domain elsewhere, thats okay, too, because Bluehost will make it easy to transfer your existing domain during the setup process.)</p>
<h3 id="set-up-blog-hosting">Set up blog hosting</h3>
<p>Once youve decided on a domain name, youll need to set up hosting for your blog. While WordPress itself is free (see Step 2 below), you need a reliable place to host your WordPress blog (your blog needs to be on a server somewhere on the Internet).</p>
<p>For hosting, we recommend <a href="https://bluehost.sjv.io/Vy9MJJ" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Bluehost</a> for several reasons:</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>We Use Bluehost.</strong> We personally use Bluehost to host <em>The Minimalists</em>. If you recommend a company, you better be willing to use their product yourself. We also use them to host several other websites of ours.</li>
<li><strong>Great Pricing.</strong> TheMinimalists.com is a Bluehost affiliate partner, which means that in addition to using their service, we also receive a commission for referring new customers. To be fair, though, we would still use Bluehost even if we werent an affiliateweve used them for a long time. Ergo, we dont recommend Bluehost just because were an affiliate (every hosting company offers a similar affiliate program); we recommend Bluehost because they are the best, most reliable option. Plus, because were a partner, Bluehost offers a more than 50% discount for <em>The Minimalists</em> readers: only <a href="https://bluehost.sjv.io/Vy9MJJ" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">$2.95 a month</a> for the first year.</li>
<li><strong>Free Domain.</strong> When you sign up for hosting, Bluehost will give you a free domain name, which allows you to avoid the upfront and recurring fees associated with purchasing a domain on your own. If youve already purchased your own domain name, dont worry; you can still use your domain with Bluehost (its just one extra step).</li>
<li><strong>Money-Back Guarantee.</strong> Bluehost offers a 30-day money-back guarantee, so theres no risk if you change your mind.</li>
<li><strong>Reliability.</strong> Bluehosts facilities are world class. They have their own custom-built 20,000-square-foot datacenter with enough backup generators to power a city.</li>
<li><strong>Friends &amp; Family.</strong><p><a href="https://www.heavytowingtampa.com/">heavy duty towing tampa</a> Many of our friends and family also use Bluehost to host their blogs.</li>
</ul>
<p>Now that youre ready to get started, go to <a href="https://bluehost.sjv.io/Vy9MJJ" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Bluehost</a> and click the <strong>Get Started Now</strong> button.</p>
<p><a href="https://bluehost.sjv.io/Vy9MJJ" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 1 - Get Started Now" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-1-Get-Started-Now.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-1-Get-Started-Now.jpg" alt="Step 1 - Get Started Now" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></a></p>
<p>Next choose your hosting plan.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 1 - Choose your blog hosting" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-1-Choose-your-blog-hosting.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-1-Choose-your-blog-hosting.jpg" alt="Step 1 - Choose your blog hosting" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<p>Youll see that prices range from $3 to $6 per month, depending on whether you want a basic, single blog hosting plan or a more robust plan that allows you to create multiple blogs.<p><a href="https://www.heavytowingtampa.com/">heavy towing tampa</a></p>
<div class="note">Note: Because were an affiliate partner, Bluehost offers a special price for The Minimalists readers: only <a href="https://bluehost.sjv.io/Vy9MJJ" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">only $2.95 a month</a> for the first year. Thats a significant discount.</div>
<p>Once you select your plan youll choose or enter your domain name.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 1 - Sign Up Now" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-1-Sign-up-now.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-1-Sign-up-now.jpg" alt="Step 1 - Sign Up Now" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<p>If you dont own a domain name simply enter your desired blog name into the <strong>New Domain</strong> box.</p>
<p>If youve already own a domain name simply enter that into the <strong>I have a domain name</strong> box.</p>
<p>Click <strong>Next</strong>.</p>
<p>Finally create your blogging account.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 1 - Create Your Account" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-1-Create-Your-Account.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-1-Create-Your-Account.jpg" alt="Step 1 - Create Your Account" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<p>And click <strong>Create your password</strong> to complete your blog hosting setup.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 1 - Welcome to Bluehost" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-1-Welcome-to-Bluehost.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-1-Welcome-to-Bluehost.jpg" alt="Step 1 - Welcome to Bluehost" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<p>Just like that youve nearly become a blogger!</p>
<hr class="narrow">

<div class="content-upgrade-full" id="ebook">
<img src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20184%20239&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" width="184" height="239" alt="Starting a Blog" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/how-to-start-a-blog.png"><noscript><img src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/how-to-start-a-blog.png" width="184" height="239" alt="Starting a Blog" /></noscript>

<hr class="narrow">
<h2 id="start-a-blog-step2" class="start-a-blog-step"><span class="step-highlight">Step 2</span> Start your blog by adding WordPress</h2>
<p>Next you will install WordPress, which is free. Dont let the word install intimidate you, though. Its much easier than it sounds and Bluehost does all the work for you.</p>
<div id="start-fast-2" class="quick-start">
<h3>Blogging Quick Start  Step 2</h3>
<p>Next youll install WordPress.</p>
<ol>
<li>Click the <strong><em>Log In</em></strong> button.</li>
<li>Click <strong><em>Skip This Step</em></strong> on the Pick a theme screen.</li>
<li>WordPress is now installed, click <strong><em>Start Building</em></strong> to go to your dashboard.</li>
</ol>
<p><a href="https://www.theminimalists.com/blog/#start-fast-3">Click here</a> to jump to the next step.</p>
</div>
<p>To begin simply click <strong>Log In</strong>.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 2 - Log In" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-2-Log-In.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-2-Log-In.jpg" alt="Step 2 - Log In" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<p>Bluehost provides several blog design options, but simply scroll to the bottom and click <strong>Skip This Step</strong> (youll see why in a moment).</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 2 - Click Skip This Step" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-2-Click-Skip-This-Step.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-2-Click-Skip-This-Step.jpg" alt="Step 2 - Click Skip This Step" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<p>WordPress is now installed. Simply click <strong>Start Building</strong> to go to your new blogging dashboard and continue to Step 3.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 2 - Click Start Building" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-2-Click-Start-Building.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-2-Click-Start-Building.jpg" alt="Step 2 - Click Start Building" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<h2 id="start-a-blog-step3" class="start-a-blog-step"><span class="step-highlight">Step 3</span> Pick a simple theme to make your blog your own</h2>
<p>A theme allows you to pick a design for your blog without the need for coding expertise or design knowledge. In other words, a&nbsp;good&nbsp;theme helps you to design your blog exactly how&nbsp;<em>you</em>&nbsp;want it to look. If youre not a coder (Im certainly not a coder), then a theme makes the design work a million times easier.</p>
<div id="start-fast-3" class="quick-start">
<h3>Blogging Quick Start  Step 3</h3>
<p>Next youll choose and install your blogs WordPress theme.</p>
<ol>
<li>Go to <a href="https://bylt.co/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">BYLT</a>.</li>
<li><strong><em>Purchase</em></strong> the theme that fits your style (we use the tru Theme).</li>
<li><strong><em>Download</em></strong> and save your themes .zip file to your Desktop.</li>
<li>Return to your WordPress dashboard and go to <strong><em>Appearance &gt; Themes</em></strong>.</li>
<li>Click <strong><em>Upload</em></strong> and then <strong><em>Upload Theme</em></strong>.</li>
<li>Click <strong><em>Choose File</em></strong>, select your theme .zip file, and click <strong><em>Install Now</em></strong>.</li>
<li>Click <strong><em>Activate</em></strong>.</li>
</ol>
<p><a href="https://www.theminimalists.com/blog/#start-fast-4">Click here</a> to jump to the next step.</p>
</div>
<p>Our blog design is from BYLT, a platform created by our good friends at SPYR. They have several beautiful, simple WordPress themes to choose from, and,&nbsp;in fact, you can purchase the same theme we use if you like.</p>
<p>Simply go to <a href="http://bylt.co/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">BYLT</a> and find the minimalist WordPress theme that best fits your desired aesthetic. Their themes are feature-rich; plus, once you buy your theme, you will have the same team supporting your work that we trust to support ours.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" style="border: 1px solid #eee;" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%201200%20809&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 3 - Blog Designs" width="1200" height="809" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/bylt-minimalist-wordpress-themes.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" style="border: 1px solid #eee;" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/bylt-minimalist-wordpress-themes.jpg" alt="Step 3 - Blog Designs" width="1200" height="809" /></noscript></p>
<p>Once you purchase your theme youll be able to download your WordPress theme (a .zip file) from your <a href="https://bylt.co/dashboard" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">BYLT Dashboard</a>. Save this file to your Desktop because youll need to upload it to WordPress in just a moment.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" style="border: 1px solid #eee;" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%201200%20571&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 3 - Download a Blog Theme" width="1200" height="571" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/BYLT-Dashboard.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" style="border: 1px solid #eee;" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/BYLT-Dashboard.jpg" alt="Step 3 - Download a Blog Theme" width="1200" height="571" /></noscript></p>
<p>Remember how easy it was to install WordPress? Well installing your blog theme is just as simple.</p>
<p>First return to your WordPress Dashboard.</p>
<p>You should already be logged in, but whenever you are signed out go to <a href="https://my.bluehost.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">my.bluehost.com</a>, enter your new domain name (or username), your password, and click <strong>Submit</strong>.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 3 - Log In to Blog" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-Log-In-to-Blog.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-Log-In-to-Blog.jpg" alt="Step 3 - Log In to Blog" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<p>From here, go to <strong>My Sites</strong> and click on <strong>Log in to WordPress</strong>.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 3 - My Sites" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-My-Sites.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-My-Sites.jpg" alt="Step 3 - My Sites" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<p>Next, in your WordPress dashboard, go to <strong>Appearance &gt; Themes</strong>.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 3 - Appearance &gt; Themes" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-Appearance-Themes.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-Appearance-Themes.jpg" alt="Step 3 - Appearance &gt; Themes" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<p>Next, click the <strong>Upload</strong> button.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 3 - Upload Blog Design" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-Upload-Blog-Design.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-Upload-Blog-Design.jpg" alt="Step 3 - Upload Blog Design" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<p>Then, click the <strong>Upload Theme</strong> button followed by the <strong>Choose File</strong> button.</p>
<p>Find the .zip file you downloaded from your BYLT Dashboard&nbsp;(this is your theme file) and click <strong>Install Now</strong> to install your new simple blog design.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 3 - Install Blog Theme" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-Install-Blog-Theme.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-Install-Blog-Theme.jpg" alt="Step 3 - Install Blog Theme" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<p>Finally, click <strong>Activate</strong> and your blog theme is installed.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%20800%20500&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 3 - Activate Blog Theme" width="800" height="500" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-Activate-Blog-Theme.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-3-Activate-Blog-Theme.jpg" alt="Step 3 - Activate Blog Theme" width="800" height="500" /></noscript></p>
<h2 id="start-a-blog-step4" class="start-a-blog-step"><span class="step-highlight">Step 4</span> Add two key blogging plugins to find your readers and track stats</h2>
<p>Plugins are third-party appendages&nbsp;that add additional functionality to your blog.</p>
<div id="start-fast-4" class="quick-start">
<h3>Blogging Quick Start  Step 4</h3>
<p>In the final setup step youll install two plugins that will improve your blogs features.</p>
<ol>
<li>In your WordPress Dashboard go to <strong>Plugins &gt; Add New</strong>.</li>
<li>Search for <strong>Yoast SEO</strong>. Click <strong>Install Now</strong> followed by <strong>Activate</strong>.</li>
<li>Click the <strong>Add New</strong> button to add one more plugin.</li>
<li>Search for <strong>MonsterInsights</strong> and click <strong>Install Now</strong> followed by <strong>Activate</strong>.</li>
<li>Click the <strong>Launch the Wizard!</strong> button to configure MonsterInsights.</li>
</ol>
<p><a href="https://www.theminimalists.com/blog/#start-a-blog-step5">Click here</a> to jump to the next step.</p>
</div>
<p>Its&nbsp;best to keep your number of blog plugins to a minimum and install only the best ones, because too many pluginsas well as unreliable pluginscan slow down your site. We use very few plugins at <em>The Minimalists</em>.</p>
<p>In this section youll install and activate the following <em>free</em> plugins:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="http://wordpress.org/plugins/wordpress-seo/"><strong>Yoast SEO</strong></a>&nbsp;is the defacto standard SEO plugin for WordPress. For details and everything youd ever want to know about WordPress SEO read&nbsp;<a href="https://yoast.com/articles/wordpress-seo/">Yoasts Definitive SEO Guide</a>.</li>
<li><a href="http://wordpress.org/plugins/google-analytics-for-wordpress/"><strong>Google Analytics for WordPress by MonsterInsights</strong></a>&nbsp;allows you to track your blogs traffic easily and with lots of interesting data: overall traffic, traffic sources, views per author &amp; category, automatic tracking of outbound clicks and pageviews.</li>
</ul>
<p>In your WordPress dashboard go to&nbsp;<strong>Plugins &gt; Add New</strong>.</p>
<p>Search for <strong>Yoast SEO</strong>.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%201140%20461&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 4 - Install Yoast SEO" width="1140" height="461" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-4-Install-Yoast-SEO.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-4-Install-Yoast-SEO.jpg" alt="Step 4 - Install Yoast SEO" width="1140" height="461" /></noscript></p>
<p>Then click <strong>Install Now</strong> followed by <strong>Activate</strong> and your blog will immediately have improved SEO.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%201142%20460&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 4 - Activate Yoast SEO" width="1142" height="460" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-4-Activate-Yoast-SEO.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-4-Activate-Yoast-SEO.jpg" alt="Step 4 - Activate Yoast SEO" width="1142" height="460" /></noscript></p>
<p>Next search for <strong>MonsterInsights</strong>.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%201141%20505&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 4 - Install MonsterInsights" width="1141" height="505" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-4-Install-MonsterInsights.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-4-Install-MonsterInsights.jpg" alt="Step 4 - Install MonsterInsights" width="1141" height="505" /></noscript></p>
<p>Then click <strong>Install Now</strong> followed by <strong>Activate</strong>.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%201138%20504&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 4 - Activate MonsterInsights" width="1138" height="504" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-4-Activate-MonsterInsights.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-4-Activate-MonsterInsights.jpg" alt="Step 4 - Activate MonsterInsights" width="1138" height="504" /></noscript></p>
<p>Next click <strong>Launch the Wizard!</strong> and follow the steps to complete the MonsterInsights setup.</p>
<p><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg%20xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;%20viewBox=&#39;0%200%201138%20754&#39;%3E%3C/svg%3E" alt="Step 4 - Click Launch the Wizard!" width="1138" height="754" data-lazy-src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-4-Click-Launch-the-Wizard.jpg"><noscript><img decoding="async" class="aligncenter" src="https://www.theminimalists.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/Step-4-Click-Launch-the-Wizard.jpg" alt="Step 4 - Click Launch the Wizard!" width="1138" height="754" /></noscript></p>
<p>Finally, so people can receive our blog posts via email, we established a free <a href="http://feedburner.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Feedburner</a>&nbsp;account. For a more feature-rich email-subscription service we recommend <a href="https://www.theminimalists.com/constant-contact/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Constant Contact</a> (affiliate link). (By the way, if you dont already, <a href="http://theminimalists.email/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">subscribe to&nbsp;<em>The Minimalists</em> blog via email</a>.)</p>
<h2 id="start-a-blog-step5" class="start-a-blog-step"><span class="step-highlight">Step 5</span> Write compelling content to create a blog that your readers love</h2>
<p>Congratulations! You started a blog, and now its time to start blogging. This is where the fun begins.</p>
<p>Now that you have your own blog, you get to make it <em>yours</em>; you get to turn your vision into a reality.</p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Content</strong>. Start writing and publishing the content for your basic pages: create an About Page, Contact Page, Start Here Page, and any other page you want in the header of your new blog.</li>
<li><strong>Photo</strong>. Add a photo of yourself (pro tip: you can start with a well-lit selfie, but when you get a chance, get some professional photos taken; theyre well worth the cost because people identify with other people more than they identify with logos).</li>
<li><strong>Logo</strong>. Create a basic logo using a program like InDesign, Photoshop, or a text editor (note: even though we have no design skills, we were able to use Apples Pages application to create our simple logo after downloading some <a href="http://designshack.net/articles/graphics/10-awesome-places-to-download-free-vector-art/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">free vector art</a>&nbsp;and choosing the typeface that best suited our aesthetic). Or you can hire someone like <a href="http://99designs.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">99designs</a> or <a href="https://spyr.me/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">SPYR</a> to design a professional logo.</li>
<li><strong>Images</strong>. Spice up your blog posts with high-quality stock photos and images: <a href="http://pjrvs.com/photos/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Paul Jarvis</a> (free), <a href="http://unsplash.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Unsplash</a> (free), <a href="http://www.loc.gov/pictures/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Library of Congress</a> (free),&nbsp;<a href="http://www.istockphoto.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">iStock</a>&nbsp;(fee-based), <a href="http://www.shutterstock.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Shutterstock</a> (fee-based).</li>
<li><strong>Comments</strong>. Determine whether or not you want comments on your blog; they are often a useful way to receive feedback and directly engage with your readers.</li>
<li><strong>Social</strong>. Establish a social media presence on <a href="https://twitter.com/theminimalists" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Twitter</a>, <a href="https://facebook.com/theminimalists" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Facebook</a>, or <a href="https://instagram.com/theminimalists" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Instagram</a> (or all three).</li>
<li><strong>Publish</strong>. Start writing new blog posts. Publish at least once a week, especially when first starting a blog, so you can build an audience. Below youll also find 20 blogging tips to improve your writing in the <a href="https://www.theminimalists.com/blog/#how-to-blog">How to Blog</a> section, as well as 15 reasons you should start a blog and 3 reasons <em>not</em> to start a blog.</li>
</ul>
<p>We hope you have loads of fun expressing yourself on your new blog. Were certain it will be a huge growth experience for you during the coming months. You have now officially become a blogger. Wherever youre going, make sure you enjoy the journey ahead.</p>
<hr class="narrow">
<h2 id="how-to-blog">How to Blog: 20 Blogging Tips to Improve Your Writing</h2>
<p>We receive many emails asking how to blog, about blog topics, and about creating meaningful content. The bulk of this essay explained how to start a blog, but thats just the initial step. Now its time to start writing and publishing your content.</p>
<p>Here, to answer the frequently asked How can a beginner start blogging?, are 20 tips for beginners on <em>how to blog</em>.</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Find Your Niche</strong>. You neednt have a niche, but it helps. When learning how to be a blogger, its important to ask yourself what youre passionate about. Running? Cooking? Being a parent? Have you found your passion? If so, whatever it is, write about that. If not, then you must first <a href="http://calnewport.com/blog/2014/08/24/the-nuanced-road-to-passion-a-career-case-study/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">find your passion</a>.Note: We generally recommend that people dont start a blog about minimalism or keto or any other heavily saturated topic. But what we really mean when we say this is: dont create a blog about something unless you have a unique perspective. If youve embraced simple living and have a unique perspective, then by all means have at it.</li>
<li><strong>Define Your Ideal Readers</strong>. Once youve found your niche, you need to know who will be reading your blog. For example, we blog&nbsp;about living a meaningful life with less. Thus, our ideal readers are people who are interested in exploring minimalism so they can clear the path toward more meaningful lives.If you want to write about your newborn baby growing up, thats wonderful: your ideal readers are probably your friends and family. If you want to write about restoring classic cars, thats cool, too. Tailor your writing to your readers (whether its your family or local community or whoever else will read your blog).</li>
<li><strong>Add Value</strong>. Your blog must add value to its readers lives. You want to help people solve problems. This is the only way you will get great quality readers to your site (and keep them coming back).Adding value is the only way to get someones long-term buy-in. We both learned this after a decade of leading and managing people in the corporate world. With everything you write, its worth asking: Is this adding value?</li>
<li><strong>Be Original</strong>. Yes, there are other blogs out there about the same thing you want to write about. Question: So why is your blog different? Answer: Because of <em>you</em>. <em>You</em> are what makes <em>your</em> blog different. Its about <em>your</em> perspective, <em>your</em> creativity, the value&nbsp;<em>you</em> add.</li>
<li><strong>Be Interesting</strong>. Write interesting&nbsp;blog posts. Especially if you want people to share it with others.</li>
<li><strong>Be Yourself</strong>. Part of being interesting is telling <em>your</em> story. Every person is unique, and your story is an important one. The important part of storytelling, however, is removing the superfluous details that make the story uninteresting. A great storyteller removes 99% of what really happensthe absorptive detailsand leaves the interesting 1% for the reader.</li>
<li><strong>Be Honest</strong>. Your blog needs to be authenticit needs to <em>feel</em> realif you want people to read it. You can be your blog, or your blog can be you. That is, do you really embody the stuff you write about? If not, people will see through it.Be the change you want to see in the world, is the famous Gandhi quote. Perhaps bloggers should build the blog they want to write for the world.</li>
<li><strong>Transparency</strong>. Being transparent is different from being honest. You neednt share every detail about your life just for the sake of being honest.Always be honest, and be transparent when it adds value to what youre writing. (Because everything we write must serve the greater good, you wont ever see pictures of us using the restroomthats simply not relevant.)</li>
<li><strong>Time</strong>. Once youve learned how to start a blog, youll learn that blogging takes a lot of time, especially if youre as neurotic as we are.That said, once you have your design set up, dont tweak it too much. Instead, spend the time on your writing.</li>
<li><strong>Vision</strong>. The reason our site design looks good is because we have a great <a href="https://bluehost.sjv.io/Vy9MJJ" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">host</a>, we have a great <a href="https://bylt.co/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">theme</a>, and, most important, we had a vision of how we wanted our blog to look.Once we had the vision, we worked hard to make that vision a reality. (Note: neither of us had any design experience before starting a blog.) Its hard to create a beautiful blog if you dont know what you want it to look like.</li>
<li><strong>Find Your Voice</strong>. Over time, good writers discover their voice and their writing tends to develop a certain flow, one that is appealing to their readers. Finding your voice makes your writing feel more alive, more real, more urgent. For additional reading, check out our blog post about <a href="https://www.theminimalists.com/voice/">Finding Your Voice</a>.</li>
<li><strong><em>We</em> Instead of <em>You</em></strong>. Use the first-person plural when possible. Statements of <em>we</em> and <em>our</em> are more powerful than <em>you</em> and <em>your</em>, especially when talking about negative behaviors or tendencies. The first person comes off as far less accusatory. Think of it this way: were writing peer-to-peerwe are not gods.</li>
<li><strong>When to Post</strong>. Question: When is the best day and time to publish a blog post? Answer: It doesnt really matter. We dont adhere to a particular time-of-day schedule, but we do publish at least once a week because consistency is important. You neednt get bogged down in the details, though.</li>
<li><strong>Social Media</strong>. Yes, we recommend using <a href="https://twitter.com/theminimalists" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Twitter</a>, <a href="https://facebook.com/theminimalists" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Facebook</a>, and <a href="https://instagram.com/theminimalists" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Instagram</a> to help connect with your audience and other bloggers, but dont get too caught up in it. Focus on the writing first, social media thereafter.</li>
<li><strong>Ignore Negative Criticism and Stupidity</strong>. Sure, we get a lot of negative comments and stupid questions from ignorant people who arent really our readers (Youre not real minimalists!).We call these people <a href="https://theminimalists.com/seagulls">seagulls</a>: They fly in, crap on your site, and fly away. But we pay them no mind, because we didnt start our blog for them. Delete their comment and move on.</li>
<li><strong>Research</strong>. Spend time researching what youre writing about. The reason we are able to use so many helpful, relevant links in our essays is because we put in the time to research our topics.</li>
<li><strong>Keep It Simple</strong>. This is where minimalism can be applied to starting any blog, irrespective of its genre. No need to place superfluous advertisements or widgets all over your site. Stick to the basics and remove anything you dont needremove anything that doesnt add value.</li>
<li><strong>Picture</strong>. Put a picture of yourself on your blog. People like to see the face of the person whos writing the blog. If two goofy guys from Dayton, Ohio arent too afraid to put their pictures on their site, then you have nothing to worry about.</li>
<li><strong>Comments</strong>. If youre going to have comments on your site, then read <a href="http://www.unmarketing.com/2010/12/07/the-five-words-that-kill-your-blog/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">The Five Words That Kill Your Blog</a> by Scott Stratten.</li>
<li><strong>Live Your Life</strong>. Youre starting a blog about your life (or about certain aspects of your life, at least), so you still need to live your life. There are things that we always put before blogging: exercise, health, relationships, experiences, personal growth, contribution. Simply put, live a life worth writing about.</li>
</ol>
<hr class="narrow">
<h2 id="reasons">15 Reasons You Should Start a Blog</h2>
<p>We were inspired to research and write this blog post after reading Joshua Beckers <a href="https://www.becomingminimalist.com/15-reasons-i-think-you-should-blog/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">15 Reasons I Think You Should Blog</a>, in which he discusses 15 great reasons <em>why</em> you should start a blog.</p>
<p><em>Why</em> is the keyword here. Crucially, Becker writes about the <em>purpose</em> of blogging, not just how to start a blog. Thats what many of these other blogs about blogging seem to miss: they miss the <em>purpose</em>the <em>why</em> behind starting a blog.</p>
<p>Here is a summary of our three favorite reasons from Beckers list:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Youll become a better writer</strong>. At its core, writing is communication. It is about recording thoughts on paper and compelling others to agree with them, writes Becker. To that end, writing (just like every other form of communication that has ever existed) improves with practice. Blogging will not force you to become a better writer, itll just happen as you do it. And becoming a better writer holds important benefits for the rest of your lifewhether you are creating a book, a presentation, a resume, or an anniversary card for your spouse. Spot on! Writing blog posts is not only a great way to improve your blog writing, its a wonderful chance to improve everything you writefrom business emails and text messages to that novel youve been dreaming of penning.</li>
<li><strong>Youll meet new people</strong>. Whether it be through comments, emails, or social media, you may be surprised at how quickly you meet people online, writes Becker. Thats true! The Minimalists blog is responsible for many of the most important relationships Ive developed over the past decadelong-term business and personal relationships birthed from this very blog</li>
<li><strong>Youll become more confident</strong>. Blogging will help you discover more confidence in your life, writes Becker. You will quickly realize that you do live an important life with a unique view and have something to offer others. So true! Writing helps us better understand the lives we live and the consequences of our actions.</li>
</ol>
<hr class="narrow">
<h2 id="do-not-start-a-blog">3 Reasons You Should Not Start a Blog</h2>
<p>So now you have 15 reasons <em>why</em> you should start a blog, and weve shown you <em>how</em> to start a blog, step-by-step, based on our personal experience.</p>
<p>But after giving you those detailed instructions, which could save you hundreds of hours of wasted time, we also want to give you some good reasons why you should <em>not</em> start a blog. (Keep in mind that these reasons are just our opinions, and we do not pretend to offer them up as a collection of empirical blogging maxims.)</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Money</strong>. You should not start a blog to make money. We need to get that out of the way first. If your primary objective is to replace your full-time income from blogging, forget about it. It doesnt work that way.Do you think that Jimi Hendrix picked up his first guitar so he could supplement his income? No, he didnt. Rather, he did it for the love of it, for the joy and fulfillment he received, and the income came thereaftermuch later actually.</li>
<li><strong>Notoriety</strong>. Dont plan on getting Internet famous right away. Not every site grows as fast as ours did, but thats okay. The truth is that we kind of got lucky. We found a great domain name, we cobbled together a logo and site design that people liked, we write fairly well, and our content connected with people in a unique way.We didnt start this site to become famous, though. Thatd be ridiculous. We started this site to become bloggers and share a message. Our popularity came as a surprise to us, and it was a result of a little luck and a lot of hard, passionate work.</li>
<li><strong>Traffic</strong>. Not all traffic is <a href="https://www.theminimalists.com/blogging/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">good traffic</a>, so dont worry about getting thousands of readers right away. Spend your time producing meaningful creations and eventually the audience will show up if you are helping people solve problems. In other words, focus on adding value, not increasing traffic.</li>
</ol>
<p>The funny thing is that all these things <em>can</em> happen. You <em>could</em> make a full-time income from building a blog. We do it, <a href="https://fizzle.co/sparkline/grow-email-list" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Corbett Barr</a> does it, and so do many others. And you <em>could</em> become an Internet famous blogger like <a href="https://zenhabits.net/money-integrity/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Leo Babauta</a> or <a href="https://chrisbrogan.com/blogging-isnt-dead/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Chris Brogan</a>.</p>
<p>But if these are the sole reasons you start blogging, youll be miserable because it will seem like a job. And if it feels like a job, you wont be passionate about it, so youll either hate it or fall flat on your face (or both).</p>
<p>Instead, become a blogger and write because youre passionate about it</p>
<hr class="narrow">
<h2 id="resources">4 Blogging Resources</h2>
<p>If you want to learn more about blogging, publishing, writing, and SEO, then check out these additional resources:</p>
<ul>

</ul>
